#### Basecoating

The initial layer of paint applied to a miniature, providing the fundamental color upon which further detail can be added.

**Tags:** painting technique, hobby, miniatures

**Related:** Citadel Paint System

---

### Level 1 - Basic

#### Firestorm Attack Dice Placement

The process of placing six dice numbered 1 to 6 at least 9 inches apart on the battlefield to represent Firestorm attack locations.

**Also known as:** Firestorm Dice Placement

**Tags:** game mechanic, dice placement, Planetstrike

**Prerequisites:** Firestorm Attack

**Related:** Targeting Jammers Stratagem

---

#### Garrisoning Bastions

Defender infantry units can occupy Bastions (up to 20 models), generally unable to act or be affected except they can shoot during the Shooting phase and must disembark if Bastions are destroyed, with a chance to be crushed by rubble.

**Tags:** defense, unit positioning, planetary assault

**Prerequisites:** INFANTRY Model

**Related:** Bastions

---

#### Deployment

The process of setting up models on the battlefield in designated deployment zones according to turn order and positional restrictions.

**Also known as:** Army Setup

**Tags:** game setup, battlefield, Phase, game phase, setup, strategy, Setup Phase, Gameplay

**Prerequisites:** Turn

**Related:** Transport (Deployment), Reserve Units, Landing Zone, Battle Round Phases, Concealed Deployment

---

#### Active Tactical Objectives

Tactical Objectives that have been generated and remain in play until achieved or discarded by the player.

**Tags:** game state, objectives

**Prerequisites:** Discarding Tactical Objectives

**Related:** Tactical Objectives

---

#### Tactical Objective Markers

Numbered objective markers (1–6) placed on the battlefield to represent Tactical Objectives that players compete to achieve.

**Also known as:** Tactical Objective

**Tags:** game components, objectives

**Prerequisites:** Objective Marker Placement

**Related:** Objective Marker

---

#### Tactical Objectives

Optional or mandatory goals generated and achieved during the game that grant victory points, which vary in type and can have special rules depending on the mission variation.

**Also known as:** Tactical Objective Markers, Secret Tactical Objectives

**Tags:** game objectives, mission-specific, objectives, victory points, gameplay, game mechanics, Warhammer 40k, Warhammer 40,000, Missions

**Prerequisites:** Control (in Tactical Objectives)

**Related:** Active Tactical Objectives, Maelstrom of War Missions, Objective Marker, Dice

---

#### Minor Victory

A game result awarded to the player whose model is closest to the Relic at game end if no model carries it, or a tie if models are equally close.

**Tags:** game results, victory conditions, Victory Condition, Gameplay, Warhammer 40,000

**Prerequisites:** Relic

**Related:** Tactical Priority

---

#### Relic Carrier

An infantry model that has picked up the Relic and moves it; subject to restrictions such as limited movement and inability to embark transports or leave the battlefield.

**Tags:** unit status, scenario rules

**Prerequisites:** Relic

**Related:** Adeptus Astartes Chapters

---

#### Deployment Zone

A designated area on the battlefield where a player must set up their units before the battle begins, defined by mission setup and influenced by the placement of objective markers.

**Also known as:** Deployment Area

**Tags:** game setup, battlefield areas, battlefield, positioning, Warhammer 40k, game phase, strategy, Warhammer 40,000, Gameplay Element, Setup Phase, deployment, battlefield positioning

**Prerequisites:** Linebreaker

**Related:** Objective Marker Placement

---

#### Slay the Warlord

A victory condition granting one victory point if the enemy Warlord unit is destroyed; grants an additional point if the Warlord is a Heavy Support unit.

**Tags:** victory conditions, scoring, victory condition, combat, objectives, Warhammer 40k, unit destruction, game objectives

**Prerequisites:** Warlord

**Related:** Adeptus Astartes

---

#### Destroy the Big Guns

A victory condition scoring one victory point for each enemy Heavy Support unit completely destroyed.

**Tags:** victory conditions, scoring

**Prerequisites:** Heavy Support Unit

---

#### Control (of an Objective Marker)

Having more models within 3 inches of the objective marker's center than the opponent; for Heavy Support units, control may be granted by presence of only one player's Heavy Support models within that range.

**Tags:** game mechanics, scoring

**Prerequisites:** Heavy Support Unit

**Related:** Control (in Tactical Objectives)

---

#### Power Level

A numerical rating assigned to Warhammer 40,000 miniatures used to approximate their overall strength for balancing armies in open play or matched play games.

**Also known as:** Power Rating

**Tags:** Warhammer 40,000, Gameplay, Balancing, game mechanics, army building, army composition, game balance, game mechanic, balance, army, Gameplay Mechanic, Ranking, army stats

**Prerequisites:** Miniatures

---

#### Morale Test

A roll made by a player to determine if a unit that lost models in the turn suffers fleeing models, where the dice roll plus slain models is compared against the unit’s highest Leadership characteristic.

**Also known as:** Morale Checks

**Tags:** Game Mechanic, Morale, Psychological, psychological check, Test, Gameplay Mechanic

**Prerequisites:** Leadership Characteristic

**Related:** Fleeing, Leadership Characteristic

---

#### Weapon Skill

A characteristic that determines the dice roll needed for a close combat attack to hit, e.g., 3+ means hitting on a roll of 3 or higher.

**Also known as:** WS

**Tags:** Unit Characteristic, Combat, unit attribute, combat stat

**Prerequisites:** Plague Knives

---

#### Piling In

The movement allowing models within a unit to move up to 3" closer to the nearest enemy model after a fight to maintain engagement.

**Tags:** Movement, Fight Phase, Close Combat

**Prerequisites:** Fight Phase

**Related:** Adeptus Astartes

---

#### Overwatch

An opportunity for enemy units targeted by a charge to immediately perform a shooting attack requiring a roll of 6+ to hit, ignoring normal ballistic skill and modifiers, but cannot be performed if an enemy model is within 1 inch.

**Tags:** Combat Mechanic, Shooting, reaction fire

**Prerequisites:** Charge Phase

**Related:** Adeptus Astartes

---

#### Psychic Test

A test rolled with 2D6 attempting to manifest a psychic power; if the total is equal to or greater than the power's warp charge value, the power manifests successfully.

**Also known as:** Manifest Psychic Power, Psychic Manifestation Roll

**Tags:** Game Mechanic, Psychic Phase, dice rolls, psychic powers, game mechanics

**Prerequisites:** Psychic Phase

**Related:** Psychic Powers, Warp Charge Value

---

#### Space Marines

Superhuman warrior-legions created from the geneseed of the Primarchs, serving as the Emperor’s primary military forces in the Great Crusade and beyond.

**Also known as:** Adeptus Astartes, Legiones Astartes

**Tags:** Warhammer 40,000, Faction, Warhammer 40k, military, elite troops, Military Unit, Genetic Engineering, genetics, warfare, Lore, Military Units, fictional unit, gaming, miniatures

**Prerequisites:** Geneseed

**Related:** Codex Astartes, Death Guard

---

#### D3

A random number between 1 and 3, typically simulated by rolling a six-sided die and halving the result, used for scoring variable victory points.

**Tags:** game mechanics, dice, Game Component, Randomization

**Prerequisites:** Dice Mechanics

**Related:** Dice Mechanics

---

#### Morale Phase

The Morale Phase is when units test their courage and determination after suffering losses, using their Leadership characteristic to avoid negative effects.

**Tags:** game phases, morale, combat, Gameplay Phase

**Prerequisites:** Leadership (Ld)

**Related:** Adeptus Astartes

---

#### Advancing

Advancing is an action declared during the Movement Phase where a unit moves further by rolling a dice and adding the result to the Move characteristic but sacrifices the ability to shoot or charge that turn.

**Tags:** game mechanics, movement, combat

**Prerequisites:** Battle Round Phases

**Related:** Battle Round Phases

---

#### Falling Back

Falling Back is a movement option during the Movement Phase that allows a unit within 1 inch of enemy units to move away more than 1 inch to avoid close combat, restricting further actions that turn.

**Tags:** game mechanics, movement, combat

**Prerequisites:** Battle Round Phases

**Related:** Battle Round Phases

---

#### Modifying Characteristics

Modifying Characteristics involves adjusting a model’s stats, often due to damage or special rules, using cumulative modifiers and rounding rules.

**Also known as:** Characteristic Modification

**Tags:** game mechanics, characteristics, rules

**Prerequisites:** Modifiers

**Related:** Modifiers

---

#### Battle-forged Army

An army composition method requiring organization into Detachments with structured roles, designed to add balance and strategic depth to gameplay, used primarily in narrative and matched play styles.

**Also known as:** Battleforged Army, Army List, Structured Army

**Tags:** army building, game mechanics, Warhammer 40,000, game setup, units, army organization, game rules, Warhammer 40k, Army Composition, Gameplay Preparation, game terminology, strategy, game mechanic, stratagem, Army, Gameplay, Multiplayer, Battle-forged, Detachments

**Prerequisites:** Power Rating

**Related:** Adeptus Astartes Chapters

---

#### Ballistic Skill (BS)

Ballistic Skill is a characteristic that represents a model’s accuracy with ranged weapons, determining its effectiveness in shooting attacks.

**Also known as:** Shooting Skill

**Tags:** game mechanics, characteristics, combat

**Prerequisites:** Line of Sight

**Related:** Characteristics

---

#### Advance

A movement action units may take that typically restricts their shooting ability during the same turn, often imposing hit roll penalties when firing afterward.

**Also known as:** Advancing

**Tags:** game mechanics, movement, combat restrictions

**Prerequisites:** Cover Ground

**Related:** Heavy Weapon, Assault Weapon

---

#### Roll-off

A contest where both players roll a D6, highest roll wins; ties cause repeated roll-offs until a winner emerges. This is the only circumstance where a re-roll on a re-roll is allowed.

**Also known as:** Roll off, Dice Contest

**Tags:** game mechanics, conflict resolution, dice rolls

**Prerequisites:** Roll D6

**Related:** Sequencing (Rules Order), Dice Mechanics

---

#### Re-roll

A rule allowing a player to roll certain dice a second time, but never more than once on the same die, performed before any modifiers are applied.

**Also known as:** Dice Re-roll

**Tags:** dice mechanics, game mechanics

**Prerequisites:** Roll D6

**Related:** Dice Mechanics

---

#### Astropathic Corps

The Astropathic Corps are specialized Imperial agents who use psychic communication to send messages across vast distances.

**Tags:** Warhammer 40k, Imperium, Communication, Psykers

**Prerequisites:** Psychic Powers

**Related:** Imperium, Astropath corruption, Warp-waves, Pure thought, Trance Broadcast, Sweeping Trance Reception, Sanctioning tests, Astropath, Soul Binding, Scholastica Psykana, Astropathic Communication

#### Eye of Terror

**Also known as:** Great Rift (related), Warp Storm of the Eye of Terror, Warp Rift

---

#### Crucible of War: Ambush!

A mission scenario featuring the Attacker laying a trap in dense terrain with the Defender advancing through an exposed thoroughfare, including special rules like Dawn Raid.

**Also known as:** Ambush Mission

**Tags:** mission, scenario, game mode

**Prerequisites:** Dawn Raid

**Related:** Foxholes, Traps, Night Fight Battlezone

---

#### Outflanking Reinforcements

An Attacker Stratagem allowing reinforcement units to be placed within 6" of any battlefield edge excluding the Defender’s, instead of the normal placement.

**Tags:** Stratagem, reinforcements, attacker

**Prerequisites:** Battlefield Edge

**Related:** Sustained Assault, Tactical Priority

---

#### Setup Markers

Markers placed on the battlefield to indicate where hidden or concealed units will be set up.

**Also known as:** Set-up Markers

**Tags:** deployment, game mechanics

**Prerequisites:** Spies

**Related:** Set-up Markers

---

#### Alarm

A game event triggered by a specific action that can immediately end the Attacker's turn or allow the Defender to take a special turn depending on when it arises.

**Also known as:** Alarm Raised, Alarm sounds

**Tags:** game mechanics, turn structure, game state

**Prerequisites:** Response Forces

**Related:** Sentries, Tactical Priority

#### Command Points (CP)

**Prerequisites:** Command Benefits

#### Aerial Combat

Engagements between aircraft squadrons involving bombers and fighters, playing a crucial role in controlling the skies during battle.

**Prerequisites:** Tactical Strike

**Related:** Dogfights, Bombers, Fighter Craft

---

#### Fortifications

Structures such as bastions and defense emplacements placed on the battlefield to provide cover and strategic advantages.

**Tags:** wargaming, battlefield terrain, defense, terrain, game mechanics

**Prerequisites:** Stronghold Assault

**Related:** Trench Warfare, Bunker Assault

---

#### Strategic Deadlock

A game condition from battle round 3 where the Command Point cost of all Stratagems is doubled, increasing the tactical resource expenditure.

**Tags:** game mechanics, advanced rules, Warhammer 40k

**Prerequisites:** Battle Rounds

**Related:** Flares

---

#### Malefic presence

The sustaining warp energies that allow Daemons to exist in realspace; when depleting these energies, Daemons can be banished temporarily.

**Tags:** Warhammer 40k lore, Warp energy, Daemons

**Prerequisites:** Daemon worlds

**Related:** Daemons of Chaos

---

#### Chaos Gods

Four powerful deities ruling the Realm of Chaos, embodying destructive aspects such as war, change, decay, and excess, who seek to dominate reality.

**Also known as:** Dark Gods, Ruinous Powers

**Tags:** Warhammer 40k lore, Antagonists, Cosmology, Warhammer 40k, Chaos, Warp Entities, Mythology

**Prerequisites:** Chaos cults

**Related:** Khorne — The Blood God, Tzeentch — The Changer of Ways, Nurgle — The Great Lord of Decay, Daemon Princes, Emperor, the Master of Mankind, Ruinous Powers

---

#### Chaos threat

The pervasive danger posed by Chaos forces—including the Chaos Gods, daemons, and corrupted mortals—that endangers humanity's survival.

**Tags:** Warhammer 40k lore, Threats

#### Initiative (First Turn)

Determines which player takes the first turn; chosen by the player who completes deployment first, but can be seized by the opponent rolling a 6 on a die.

**Prerequisites:** Dice roll mechanic

**Related:** Dice Mechanics

#### Reserve Roll

A dice roll at the end of each Movement phase where a unit in Reserve arrives on the battlefield if the result is 3 or higher.

**Also known as:** Reserve Dice Roll

**Tags:** game mechanic, unit deployment, movement phase, deployment, Warhammer 40,000, reserves

**Prerequisites:** Reserve Units, Rapid Drop Assault Stratagem

**Related:** Dice Mechanics

---

#### Defender

In certain open play missions, the army positioned to hold ground and resist the attacking force, often the one with the lower Power Level.

**Also known as:** Defending Army, Garrison

**Tags:** Warhammer 40,000, Gameplay, Missions, game roles, player roles, game strategy, player role, game mechanics, role, military, game role, deployment, strategy

**Prerequisites:** Hold at All Costs Mission, Death or Glory Mission

**Related:** Attacker, Foxholes, Traps, Defender’s Reserves, Rapid Reinforcements, Delayed Reserves, Sustained Assault, Decoys

---

#### Saving Throw

A defensive roll made by the target player to prevent damage, modified by the weapon’s Armour Penetration value and requiring a result equal to or greater than the target model’s Save characteristic.

**Also known as:** Save Roll

**Tags:** Combat Mechanic, Defense, defense mechanic, dice mechanics

**Prerequisites:** Save Characteristic, Armor Penetration (AP)

**Related:** Dice Mechanics

---

#### Preliminary Bombardment

A special rule wherein the Attacker rolls for each enemy unit before the game starts to inflict mortal wounds and prompt possible tactical responses like going to ground.

**Tags:** game phase, Attacker action, combat mechanics, special rules, narrative play, game mechanics, Stratagem, Attacker, special attack

**Prerequisites:** Sustained Bombardment, Going to Ground

**Related:** Dice Mechanics

---

#### Forging an Army

The process of assembling a game army for matched play that involves selection under agreed limits and organizing units into detachments conforming to Battleforged rules.

**Tags:** game mode, army building, game mechanics

**Prerequisites:** Battleforged army rules, Army Selection Methods

---

#### Spirit stones

Glowing gems formed from waystones that contain the essence of a deceased Aeldari; these stones are integrated into the wraithbone skeleton of their craftworlds, enabling the souls to live on as ghostly echoes.

**Tags:** fictional object, Aeldari technology, Warhammer 40K

**Prerequisites:** Waystones, Fall (of the Aeldari)

---

#### Craftworlds

Massive living starships made of wraithbone and psychoactive materials, serving as home and refuge for Craftworlder Aeldari.

**Also known as:** World-ships

**Tags:** spacecraft, Aeldari, biotechnology

**Prerequisites:** Wraithbone, Psychoactive materials

**Related:** Craftworld Aeldari

---

#### Primarch

Genetically-engineered superhuman sons of the Emperor, commanders of military forces and pivotal figures in the Great Crusade and Horus Heresy.

**Also known as:** Space Marine Primarch

**Tags:** Warhammer 40k, Adeptus Astartes, Genetics, military leaders, Imperium, Characters, Warhammer 40,000, Imperium Leadership

**Prerequisites:** Traitor Legions, First Founding

**Related:** Leman Russ

---

#### Transport Vehicle

A vehicle that can carry friendly units, with a listed transport capacity restricting the number and types of models embarked, providing mobility and protection.

**Tags:** unit type, game mechanic

**Prerequisites:** Disembark, Embark

**Related:** Transport Capacity, Imperium

---

#### Roll to Wound

A mechanic to determine if an attack successfully wounds a target by comparing the attacker's Strength to the target's Toughness with a required dice roll on a D6 according to a chart, where a roll of 1 always fails.

**Also known as:** Wound Roll

**Tags:** game mechanic, combat resolution, dice mechanics

**Prerequisites:** Toughness Characteristic, Strength Characteristic

---

#### Alarm (in Sabotage)

A status triggered automatically at the end of the turn when the first Sabotage attempt is made, causing the Defender to respond and enabling reserve arrivals.

**Also known as:** Alarm Called

**Tags:** game state, trigger, sabotage

**Prerequisites:** Alarm Conditions, Sabotage Attempt

---

#### Spotting Range

The distance within which a Sentry can detect an attacking unit, varying based on the Power Rating of the attacker’s unit.

**Tags:** game mechanic, Warhammer 40,000, unit detection

**Prerequisites:** Sentry, Camouflage

---

#### Defender’s Deployment Zone

A designated area on the battlefield where the Defender’s units are initially placed before the battle begins.

**Tags:** battlefield location, deployment

**Prerequisites:** The Tables Turned, Iron Discipline

**Related:** Centre of Battlefield

---

#### Eternal Strife

A perpetual cycle of conflict where continuous warfare prevents peace, leaving devastation in both physical and spiritual realms.

**Also known as:** Endless Conflict, Perpetual War

**Tags:** philosophy, warfare, fictional universe

**Prerequisites:** Conflict, Futility and Despair

**Related:** Conflict

---

#### Wars of Faith

Military campaigns declared by the Ecclesiarchy against heretics, unbelievers, or alien influences to further Imperium goals and cement religious dominance.

**Also known as:** Crusades

**Tags:** Imperium, religion, military

**Prerequisites:** Cult Imperialis, Heretics

**Related:** Cyclonic Torpedoes

---

#### Tyranid Hive Fleets

Massive, intergalactic swarms of Tyranid bio-ships that invade and consume life on prey worlds; notable fleets include Hydra, Scylla, Charybdis, and Kronus.

**Also known as:** Hive Fleets

**Tags:** Warhammer 40,000, Xenotech, Tyranids, Space Warfare, Fleets

**Prerequisites:** Shadow in the warp, Intergalactic Void

**Related:** Hive Mind, Octarius, Genestealers

---

#### Warhammer 40,000 gaming

The act of playing tabletop wargames using Warhammer 40,000 rules, where players command armies in strategic battles across varied terrain.

**Also known as:** tabletop gaming, Warhammer 40k gameplay

**Tags:** gaming, tabletop wargame, hobby

**Prerequisites:** Game types (Warhammer 40,000), Start Collecting! box

**Related:** Genestealer Cult army, Blood Angels army, Battles and warfare (Warhammer 40,000), Knight households, Warhammer 40,000 terrain

---

#### Command Points

A resource gained by organizing an army into Battle-forged Detachments that can be spent to activate Stratagems, which provide tactical advantages during gameplay.

**Also known as:** CP

**Tags:** resource, game mechanics, Warhammer 40,000, Resources, Gameplay

**Prerequisites:** Home Advantage, Battle-Forged Armies, Battleforged Detachment

---

### Level 2 - Intermediate

#### Achieving Tactical Objectives

The act of fulfilling the conditions of an active Tactical Objective, resulting in immediate victory points scored at the end of a turn.

**Tags:** game mechanics, scoring

**Prerequisites:** Active Tactical Objectives

---

#### Fleeing

When models fail a Morale test, some of them are removed from the battlefield to simulate retreat or breakdown.

**Tags:** Morale, Game Mechanic

**Prerequisites:** Morale Test

**Related:** Morale Test

---

#### D3 Damage

A random damage value from 1 to 3 inflicted by certain weapons or attacks, determined by rolling a D6 and dividing the result appropriately.

**Tags:** Damage, Randomization, Combat Mechanic

**Prerequisites:** Saving Throw

**Related:** Dice Mechanics

---

#### Hit Roll

A dice roll to determine whether an attack successfully hits a target, using Weapon Skill for melee combat instead of Ballistic Skill used in ranged attacks.

**Also known as:** To Hit Roll

**Tags:** Combat Mechanic, Shooting, combat mechanics, dice rolls, dice roll

**Prerequisites:** Weapon Skill

---

#### Warp Charge Value

The numerical value a psychic player must meet or exceed on a psychic test D6 roll to successfully manifest a power.

**Tags:** Psychic Power, Mechanic

**Prerequisites:** Psychic Test

**Related:** Psychic Test

---

#### Smite

A psychic power in Warhammer 40,000 that deals mortal wounds to enemy units on a successful psychic test.

**Also known as:** Smite Power

**Tags:** Psychic Power, Death Guard, Psychic Phase

**Prerequisites:** Psychic Test

**Related:** Psychic Powers

---

#### Space Wolves

A fiercely independent Space Marine Chapter originally created during the First Founding, known for their bold heroism, fierce combat style, and genetic heritage from their Primarch Leman Russ.

**Also known as:** Space Wolf Chapter

**Tags:** Warhammer 40k, Imperium, Units, Chapters, Space Marines, Genetics

**Prerequisites:** Primarch

**Related:** Wolf Brothers, Wulfen, Adeptus Astartes Chapters, Fenris

---

#### Chaos Spawn

Chaos Spawn are monstrous, mutant creatures created through the corrupting influence of Chaos, typically uncontrollable and used as shock troops in combat.

**Also known as:** Chaos Mutants

**Tags:** Warhammer 40k, Units, Chaos

**Prerequisites:** Eye of Terror

**Related:** Cult Uprising, Kasr Kharkovan

---

#### Concealed Deployment

A deployment method where units are set up on the battlefield discretely and hidden, preventing the Defender from using abilities that allow late arrival.

**Tags:** deployment, game mechanics, special rules, narrative play, game mechanic

**Prerequisites:** Setup Markers

**Related:** Set-up Markers, Decoys, Deployment

---

#### Infinity Circuit

A psychic network within craftworlds where the souls captured in spirit stones reside as ghostly echoes, preserving the essence of the dead Aeldari.

**Tags:** fictional construct, Aeldari culture, Warhammer 40K

**Prerequisites:** Spirit stones

---

#### Will of the Emperor

The guiding doctrine or intention interpreted by the High Lords of Terra for governing the Imperium and maintaining human dominion across the galaxy.

**Also known as:** Emperor's Will

**Tags:** Imperium governance, Philosophy, Warhammer 40k lore

**Prerequisites:** High Lords of Terra

---

#### Standard Template Construct (STC) System

An ancient technological system developed during the Age of Technology that provided templates enabling human colonies to efficiently construct anything from basic tools to advanced military hardware.

**Also known as:** STC system

**Tags:** Technology, Manufacturing, Age of Technology, Warhammer 40k lore

**Prerequisites:** Age of Strife

---

#### Cadia

Cadia is a lynchpin fortress world central to the defense of the Imperium from Chaos incursions, ultimately nearly destroyed during the Thirteenth Black Crusade.

**Also known as:** Cadian Gate, Fortress World Cadia, Lynchpin Fortress World

**Tags:** Warhammer 40k, Planets, Imperial Defense, Planet, Strategic Location, imperium defense

**Prerequisites:** Great Exodus of Cadia

**Related:** Cadian Shock Troops

---

#### Red Host

The red host is the name given to the army of Chaos forces that deploy before the Lion’s Gate in the attack on Terra.

**Tags:** Warhammer 40k, Chaos Army, Conflict

**Prerequisites:** Chaos Assault

**Related:** Blood Clouds

---

#### Damage

The actual injury inflicted on a model after a successful wound and failed save, reducing the model's wounds by the amount specified by the weapon or effect.

**Tags:** combat outcome, health reduction

**Prerequisites:** Roll to Wound

---

#### Ultima Founding

The founding of new Space Marine Chapters composed entirely of Primaris Space Marines after the resurrection of Roboute Guilliman.

**Tags:** History, Adeptus Astartes, Warhammer 40k

**Prerequisites:** Second Founding

**Related:** Adeptus Astartes Chapters

---

#### Specialized Organs (in Space Marines)

Nineteen (plus three in Primaris) bio-engineered organs implanted via gene-seed that enhance Space Marines' physical and mental capabilities.

**Tags:** Biology, Genetic Engineering, Adeptus Astartes

**Prerequisites:** Gene-Seed

**Related:** Progenoid Glands

---

#### Chapter (Adeptus Astartes)

A military unit of Space Marines organized per Codex Astartes into ten companies, each with tactical squads.

**Also known as:** Space Marine Chapter

**Tags:** Military Unit, Adeptus Astartes

**Prerequisites:** Legions

**Related:** Chapter Master, Dreadnought

---

#### Macharian Heresy

A seventy-year internal conflict following the Macharian Conquests, resolved by a coalition of over one hundred Space Marine Chapters fighting together.

**Tags:** Warhammer 40k, Civil War, Imperium of Man

**Prerequisites:** Macharian Conquests

**Related:** State of the Imperium

---

#### The Scouring

The prolonged military campaign following the Horus Heresy to eliminate traitor forces and restore the Imperium, involving widespread battles and political restructuring.

**Tags:** Warhammer 40k, Historical Event, Military Campaign

**Prerequisites:** Nova Terra Interregnum

**Related:** Traitor Legions

---

#### Senatorum Imperialis

The original ruling body of the Imperium that evolved into the High Lords of Terra, formed after the Horus Heresy to govern the Imperium.

**Also known as:** Imperial Senate, Council of Terra

**Tags:** government, Imperium, politics

**Prerequisites:** Malcador the Sigillite

---

#### Soul Binding

A sacred ritual by which Astropaths are psychically tested and bound to the Emperor's psychic might before release into service.

**Also known as:** Psychic binding ritual

**Tags:** ritual, psychic training, Imperium, Astropath, psychic powers

**Prerequisites:** Sanctioning tests

**Related:** Astropathic Corps

---

#### Reserve

Units kept off the battlefield initially that can be brought into play during specific phases under certain conditions, with rules differing for Attacker and Defender.

**Also known as:** Reserves

**Tags:** deployment, game phase, strategy, unit status, deployment phase

**Prerequisites:** Alarm (in Sabotage)

**Related:** Reserves, Forced March, Spy Model

---

#### Field Dressing Type II

An advanced dressing for severe las wounds suspected to penetrate vital organs; primarily cosmetic to conceal lethal injury and provide false comfort as death is inevitable.

**Also known as:** Type II Field Dressing for Las Wounds

**Tags:** combat medicine, wound care, field dressing

**Prerequisites:** Las Wound

---

#### Field Dressing Type I

A basic treatment for las wounds involving lightly covering the burn with the cleanest available material without breaking blisters or applying ointments.

**Also known as:** Type I Field Dressing for Las Wounds

**Tags:** combat medicine, first aid, field dressing

**Prerequisites:** Las Wound

---

#### Navigator families

Lineages possessing the Navigator gene, originally controlled by industrial cartels, that became influential forces in warp navigation by M19.

**Tags:** biology, warp travel, dynasties

**Prerequisites:** Navigator gene

**Related:** Warp Travel

---

#### Ace pilots

Highly skilled aircraft pilots capable of engaging effectively in fast-paced dogfights and strategic air battles.

**Also known as:** Aces

**Tags:** unit type, game mechanics, aerial combat

**Prerequisites:** Dogfight

---

#### Infantry

Foot soldiers able to move through urban terrain including walls, windows, doors, and portals, and benefit from special movement and cover rules inside city ruins.

**Tags:** unit type, movement, urban combat

**Prerequisites:** Core Rules

**Related:** Cadian Kasrkin, Ruined Buildings

---

#### Unification Wars

A prolonged military campaign in which the Emperor reconciled warring human factions on Terra and Mars, unifying humanity and ending internal conflicts.

**Tags:** warfare, history, unification, Warhammer 40,000 History, Emperor, Terra

**Prerequisites:** Age of Strife

---

#### Proto-hives

Massive cities constructed during overpopulation crises using advanced construction mediums, representing early examples of megastructures in human civilization.

**Tags:** urban development, construction, architecture

**Prerequisites:** Plasteel

---

#### Navis Nobilite

Terra-based organisation led by the Paternova comprising Navigator Houses (Passage-makers), responsible for providing Navigators who pilot human starships through warp space using their third eye.

**Also known as:** Navigator Houses, Passage-makers, Bearers of the Third Eye

**Tags:** Imperium Politics, Navigator Society, Warp Navigation, Warhammer 40k, Imperium, Organisations, Navigation, Mutants

**Prerequisites:** Third Eye (Navigator's Eye)

---

#### Generating Tactical Objectives

The process of creating Tactical Objectives at the start of each turn by rolling two dice (one for tens and one for digits) or drawing from a specialized deck of cards.

**Tags:** game mechanics, randomization

**Prerequisites:** Round, Tactical Objectives

**Related:** Tactical Objective Cards, New Orders (Stratagem)

---

#### Army Selection

The process of choosing which miniatures and units to include when assembling a playable force for a game of Warhammer 40,000.

**Also known as:** Army Composition, Force Building

**Tags:** Warhammer 40,000, Gameplay, Miniatures

**Prerequisites:** Power Level, Faction

---

#### Black Rage

A psychic malady afflicting Blood Angels causing them to experience apocalyptic visions and enter a berserk state of combat frenzy, historically linked to the death of Primarch Sanguinius.

**Tags:** Warhammer 40K, Psychological Effects, Space Marines

**Prerequisites:** Sanguinius, Curse of the Blood Angels

**Related:** Death Company, Blood Angels, Black armour with red crosses

---

#### Objective control

A player controls an objective marker if they have more models within 3 inches of its centre than the opponent.

**Tags:** game mechanic, territory, scoring

**Prerequisites:** Objective marker placement rules, Model

**Related:** Superior objective marker, Inferior objective marker

---

#### Units Arrival

The process by which units move from Reserve to being set on the battlefield, either through reserve rolls or automatic arrival after several turns.

**Tags:** deployment, unit mechanics

**Prerequisites:** Defender’s Deployment Zone, Attacker’s Deployment Zone

**Related:** Night Raider, Battle-Foraged Army

---

#### Dice Roll

The act of rolling dice to determine outcomes of actions or events in Warhammer 40,000 gameplay.

**Also known as:** Rolling Dice

**Tags:** Warhammer 40,000, Game Mechanics, Chance

**Prerequisites:** Core Rules, Command Re-roll

---

#### Stratagems

Tactical abilities or special actions that players can use during games by spending Command Points to influence outcomes or gain advantages.

**Also known as:** Tactics, Special Abilities

**Tags:** game mechanics, power usage, special abilities, tactics, Warhammer 40k, Warhammer 40,000, Gameplay, tactical options

**Prerequisites:** Battle-forged, Strategic Discipline, Command Points, Command Points (CP)

**Related:** New Orders (Stratagem), Command Re-roll Stratagem, Counter-Offensive Stratagem, Insane Bravery Stratagem, Command Points (CPs), Camouflage, Cut the Wires, Extra Sentries, Psychic Focus

---

### Level 3 - Advanced

#### Open Play Games

A flexible style of Warhammer 40,000 gameplay allowing the broadest choice of army selection with minimal restrictions, enabling players to field any miniatures from their collection.

**Also known as:** Open Play

**Tags:** Warhammer 40,000, Gameplay, Army Selection

**Prerequisites:** Army Selection

---

#### Wraithconstructs

Spirit stone-powered constructs or ghostly legions reanimated by Autarchs during war, representing the souls of fallen Aeldari trapped within wraithbone bodies.

**Tags:** fictional entity, Aeldari technology, Warhammer 40K

**Prerequisites:** Infinity Circuit

---

#### Hard Copies (of STC designs)

Physical reproductions of standard technological blueprints from STC systems, often copied repeatedly over generations, now considered rare and valuable.

**Also known as:** STC blueprints

**Tags:** Technology, STC system, Manufacturing

**Prerequisites:** Standard Template Construct (STC) System

---

#### Lion’s Gate

The Lion's Gate is a defensive position on Terra where the red host Chaos army deployed before launching their assault.

**Tags:** Warhammer 40k, Defensive Location, Terra

**Prerequisites:** Red Host

---

#### Lord Commander of the Imperium

The highest-ranking official within the Imperium’s military and political structure, a title held by Roboute Guilliman after the Horus Heresy.

**Also known as:** Commander of the Imperium, Formerly Warmaster

**Tags:** government, Imperium, military, Warhammer 40,000, Imperium Leadership, Military Rank

**Prerequisites:** Senatorum Imperialis

---

#### Take and Hold

A victory condition where players earn points for controlling objective markers by having more models within 3" of the centre than the opponent.

**Tags:** victory condition, objective control

**Prerequisites:** Objective control

---

#### Abhuman Races

Mutated or evolved human-descended populations that arose during the Age of Strife as a result of widespread mutations altering some human cultures.

**Tags:** evolution, mutation, biology

**Prerequisites:** Proto-hives

**Related:** Mutants

---

#### Victory Points

Points earned during battle that determine the winner; the player with the most victory points wins a major victory, with specific points awarded for breaking through deployment zones or destroying units.

**Also known as:** VP, Score

**Tags:** game objectives, scoring, game mechanics, objective, Warhammer 40k, Game Mechanic, objectives, victory condition, game outcome, Gameplay

**Prerequisites:** Achieving Tactical Objectives, First Blood

---

#### Matched Play

A competitive style of Warhammer 40,000 designed to ensure balanced and controlled gameplay through the use of Battle-forged armies and standardized missions, commonly used in tournaments and official events.

**Also known as:** Competitive Play, Matched Play Games, Tournament Play

**Tags:** Warhammer 40,000, Gameplay, Rules, game mode, competition, army building, Gameplay Style, Competitive Play, Gameplay Styles, Competitive, game styles, matched play, Competitive Gaming, Tournaments

**Prerequisites:** Mission (Warhammer 40K), Army Selection

**Related:** Battle-forged Armies

---

#### Wound

Damage points a model can suffer before being slain or destroyed; each successful damage reduces a model's wounds by one.

**Also known as:** Hit Point

**Tags:** combat stat, health, damage

**Prerequisites:** Damage, Allocate Wound

---

#### Cover Benefits

Defensive bonuses gained by infantry taking position on or behind ruins, including saving throw bonuses when stationary, and partial cover for other units when obscured.

**Tags:** defense, game mechanics, terrain interaction

**Prerequisites:** Infantry, Ruined Buildings

---

#### Wound Roll

A dice roll made after a successful hit to see if the attack causes damage, based on the relationship of the weapon’s Strength and the target’s Toughness.

**Tags:** Combat Mechanic, Damage Calculation, combat mechanics, dice rolls

**Prerequisites:** Hit Roll, Toughness, Strength (Weapon)

---

#### Faster-than-light Travel

A mode of space travel enabled by warp space allowing humans to traverse interstellar distances at speeds exceeding light speed.

**Also known as:** FTL Travel

**Tags:** Space Travel, Warp Technology, Physics

**Prerequisites:** Navis Nobilite, Warp Translation Points, Warp

---

### Level 4 - Expert

#### Victory Conditions

The criteria that determine the winner of a battle, such as slaying all enemy models for a major victory or being the last player with models on the battlefield for a heroic victory.

**Also known as:** Winning Conditions

**Tags:** game objectives, ending conditions, game rules, endgame, victory, game mechanics, win conditions, Warhammer 40k, game objective, Warhammer 40,000, battle outcomes

**Prerequisites:** Victory Points

**Related:** Draw, Major Victory

---

#### Autarch

The war leaders of the Aeldari craftworlds who command armies, including calling upon wraithconstructs in battle.

**Tags:** fictional role, Aeldari society, Warhammer 40K

**Prerequisites:** Wraithconstructs

---

#### Battle-forged Armies

Armies organized into Detachments that reflect their Faction's background and award Command Points for general and mission-specific Stratagems.

**Tags:** dynamic-expansion, query-generated

**Related:** Command Points (CPs), Matched Play

---

#### Echoes of War Missions

Missions that allow players to refight famous historical battles from Warhammer 40,000 lore.

**Tags:** dynamic-expansion, query-generated

---

#### Crucible of War Missions

A set of six adaptable missions representing classic battle types suitable for narrative gameplay.

**Tags:** dynamic-expansion, query-generated

---

#### Core Rules

The essential foundation rules for Warhammer 40,000 games, covering movement, psychic powers, shooting, charging, and fighting.

**Tags:** dynamic-expansion, query-generated

**Related:** Turn

---

#### Open Play

A free-form and adaptable way to play Warhammer 40,000 with minimal restrictions and a focus on creativity and fun.

**Tags:** dynamic-expansion, query-generated

**Related:** INFANTRY Model, Command Points (CPs)

---

#### Dark Imperium

A period marked by the creation of the Great Rift that caused massive turmoil in the Imperium, disrupting communication and causing time to pass strangely in different sectors of space.

**Tags:** dynamic-expansion, query-generated

**Prerequisites:** Great Rift (Cicatrix Maledictum)

**Related:** Battlezone: Psychic Maelstrom, Perils of the Warp Effects, The Emperor

---

#### Great Rift (Cicatrix Maledictum)

A massive warp phenomenon that split the galaxy, cutting off communication and causing the creation of the Dark Imperium era.

**Tags:** dynamic-expansion, query-generated

---

#### The Emperor

The immortal ruler of the Imperium whose physical form is preserved on the Golden Throne; his psychic will protects humanity and keeps daemonic incursions at bay.

**Tags:** dynamic-expansion, query-generated

**Related:** Perils of the Warp Effects, Dark Imperium

---

#### Great Rift

A massive, galaxy-wide warp rift that cracked reality asunder, disrupting psychic communication and causing widespread devastation across the Imperium.

**Tags:** dynamic-expansion, query-generated

**Related:** Battlezone: Psychic Maelstrom, Warp Storms, Hadex Anomaly, Eye of Terror, Astronomican

---

#### Warp Storms

Violent storms originating from the Great Rift that disrupt psychic communication and cause havoc across the galaxy, isolating worlds and preventing interstellar contact.

**Tags:** dynamic-expansion, query-generated

**Related:** Battlezone: Psychic Maelstrom, Great Rift, Astronomican

---

#### Hadex Anomaly

A region at the core of the Jericho Reach marking one endpoint of the Great Rift and its psychic fault lines across the galaxy.

**Tags:** dynamic-expansion, query-generated

**Related:** Great Rift

---

#### Eye of Terror

Previously the largest known warp rift, now overshadowed by the scale of the Great Rift.

**Tags:** dynamic-expansion, query-generated

**Related:** Great Rift

---

#### Astronomican

A psychic beacon used for interstellar communication, whose light blinked and vanished during the Great Rift, causing further isolation of Imperial worlds.

**Tags:** dynamic-expansion, query-generated

**Related:** Great Rift, Warp Storms

---

#### Astropath

Sanctioned psykers trained to send and receive telepathic messages across vast interstellar distances using the warp, often working with military and imperial organisations.

**Tags:** dynamic-expansion, query-generated

**Related:** Reserve Units, Astropath Choir

---

#### Warp Communication

The method by which Astropaths send focused telepathic messages as bolts of pure thought through the chaotic warp to communicate across vast distances, although vulnerable to interference and distortion.

**Tags:** dynamic-expansion, query-generated

**Prerequisites:** Astropath

---

#### Astropath Choir

A synchronized group of Astropaths working together to boost the power and clarity of complex warp messages over unimaginable distances.

**Tags:** dynamic-expansion, query-generated

**Related:** Astropath

---

#### Great Rift

A massive warp storm that disrupts and dims the Astronomican, the vital psychic beacon aiding warp navigation, increasing the dangers of warp travel and interstellar communication.

**Tags:** dynamic-expansion, query-generated

**Related:** Astronomican

---

#### Astronomican

A psychic beacon broadcast from Terra by a choir of psykers and focused by the Emperor's will, enabling Navigators to plot warp courses across the galaxy.

**Tags:** dynamic-expansion, query-generated

**Related:** Reserve Units, Great Rift
